1182	class PartitionNode(Node):
1183	    """
1184	    The base class for all partition nodes.
1185	    """
1186
1187	    max_num_producer_tasks = 100
1188	    max_card_of_producers_x_consumers = 4_096_000
1189
1190	    def __init__(
1191	        self,
1192	        ctx: Context,
1193	        input_deps: Tuple[Node, ...],
1194	        npartitions: int,
1195	        dimension: str = None,
1196	        nested: bool = False,
1197	        output_name: str = None,
1198	        output_path: str = None,
1199	        cpu_limit: int = 1,
1200	        memory_limit: Optional[int] = None,
1201	    ) -> None:
1202	        """
1203	        Partition the outputs of `input_deps` into n partitions.
1204
1205	        Parameters
1206	        ----------
1207	        npartitions
1208	            The dataset would be split and distributed to `npartitions` partitions.
1209	        dimension
1210	            The unique partition dimension. Required if this is a nested partition.
1211	        nested, optional
1212	            `npartitions` subpartitions are created in each existing partition of `input_deps` if true.
1213
1214	        Examples
1215	        --------
1216	        See unit tests in `test/test_partition.py`. For nested partition see `test_nested_partition`.
1217	        Why nested partition? See **5.1 Partial Partitioning** of [Advanced partitioning techniques for massively distributed computation](https://dl.acm.org/doi/10.1145/2213836.2213839).
1218	        """
1219	        assert isinstance(npartitions, int), f"npartitions is not an integer: {npartitions}"
1220	        assert dimension is None or re.match("[a-zA-Z0-9_]+", dimension), f"dimension has invalid format: {dimension}"
1221	        assert not (nested and dimension is None), f"nested partition should have dimension"
1222	        super().__init__(ctx, input_deps, output_name, output_path, cpu_limit, 0, memory_limit)
1223	        self.npartitions = npartitions
1224	        self.dimension = dimension if dimension is not None else PartitionInfo.default_dimension
1225	        self.nested = nested
1226
1227	    def __str__(self) -> str:
1228	        return super().__str__() + f", npartitions={self.npartitions}, dimension={self.dimension}, nested={self.nested}"
1229
1230	    @Node.task_factory
1231	    def create_producer_task(
1232	        self,
1233	        runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext,
1234	        input_deps: List[Task],
1235	        partition_infos: List[PartitionInfo],
1236	    ) -> PartitionProducerTask:
1237	        raise NotImplementedError
1238
1239	    @Node.task_factory
1240	    def create_consumer_task(
1241	        self,
1242	        runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext,
1243	        input_deps: List[Task],
1244	        partition_infos: List[PartitionInfo],
1245	    ) -> PartitionConsumerTask:
1246	        return PartitionConsumerTask(runtime_ctx, input_deps, partition_infos)
1247
1248	    @Node.task_factory
1249	    def create_merge_task(
1250	        self,
1251	        runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext,
1252	        input_deps: List[Task],
1253	        partition_infos: List[PartitionInfo],
1254	    ) -> MergeDataSetsTask:
1255	        return MergeDataSetsTask(runtime_ctx, input_deps, partition_infos)
1256
1257	    @Node.task_factory
1258	    def create_split_task(
1259	        self,
1260	        runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext,
1261	        input_deps: List[Task],
1262	        partition_infos: List[PartitionInfo],
1263	    ) -> SplitDataSetTask:
1264	        return SplitDataSetTask(runtime_ctx, input_deps, partition_infos)
1265
1266	    @property
1267	    def num_partitions(self) -> int:
1268	        return self.npartitions

1274	    """

1277	        self,

1288	            npartitions,
1289	            dimension,
1290	            nested=True,
1291	            cpu_limit=cpu_limit,
1292	            memory_limit=memory_limit,
1293	        )

1295	    @Node.task_factory
1296	    def create_producer_task(
1297	        self,
1298	        runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext,
1299	        input_deps: List[Task],
1300	        partition_infos: List[PartitionInfo],
1301	    ) -> RepeatPartitionProducerTask:

1303	            runtime_ctx,

1305	            partition_infos,

1307	            self.dimension,

1361	class UserPartitionedDataSourceNode(UserDefinedPartitionNode):
1362	    max_num_producer_tasks = 1

1364	    def __init__(self, ctx: Context, partitioned_datasets: List[DataSet], dimension: str = None) -> None:
1365	        assert isinstance(partitioned_datasets, Iterable) and all(isinstance(dataset, DataSet) for dataset in partitioned_datasets)

1367	            ctx,

1370	            dimension,

1372	        )

1379	class EvenlyDistributedPartitionNode(PartitionNode):
1380	    """
1381	    Evenly distribute the output files or rows of `input_deps` into n partitions.
1382	    """
1383
1384	    max_num_producer_tasks = 1
1385
1386	    def __init__(
1387	        self,
1388	        ctx: Context,
1389	        input_deps: Tuple[Node, ...],
1390	        npartitions: int,
1391	        dimension: str = None,
1392	        nested: bool = False,
1393	        *,
1394	        partition_by_rows=False,
1395	        random_shuffle=False,
1396	        output_name: str = None,
1397	        output_path: str = None,
1398	        cpu_limit: int = 1,
1399	        memory_limit: Optional[int] = None,
1400	    ) -> None:
1401	        """
1402	        Evenly distribute the output files or rows of `input_deps` into n partitions.
1403
1404	        Parameters
1405	        ----------
1406	        partition_by_rows, optional
1407	            Evenly distribute rows instead of input files into `npartitions` partitions, by default distribute by files.
1408	        random_shuffle, optional
1409	            Random shuffle the list of paths or parquet row groups (if `partition_by_rows=True`) in input datasets.
1410	        """
1411	        super().__init__(
1412	            ctx,
1413	            input_deps,
1414	            npartitions,
1415	            dimension,
1416	            nested,
1417	            output_name=output_name,
1418	            output_path=output_path,
1419	            cpu_limit=cpu_limit,
1420	            memory_limit=memory_limit,
1421	        )
1422	        self.partition_by_rows = partition_by_rows and npartitions > 1
1423	        self.random_shuffle = random_shuffle
1424
1425	    def __str__(self) -> str:
1426	        return super().__str__() + f", partition_by_rows={self.partition_by_rows}, random_shuffle={self.random_shuffle}"
1427
1428	    @Node.task_factory
1429	    def create_producer_task(
1430	        self,
1431	        runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext,
1432	        input_deps: List[Task],
1433	        partition_infos: List[PartitionInfo],
1434	    ):
1435	        return EvenlyDistributedPartitionProducerTask(
1436	            runtime_ctx,
1437	            input_deps,
1438	            partition_infos,
1439	            self.npartitions,
1440	            self.dimension,
1441	            self.partition_by_rows,
1442	            self.random_shuffle,
1443	            self.cpu_limit,
1444	            self.memory_limit,
1445	        )

1448	class LoadPartitionedDataSetNode(PartitionNode):
1449	    """
1450	    Load existing partitioned dataset (only parquet files are supported).

1456	        self,

1461	        nested: bool = False,
1462	        data_partition_column: str = None,
1463	        hive_partitioning: bool = False,
1464	        cpu_limit: int = 1,
1465	        memory_limit: Optional[int] = None,
1466	    ) -> None:

1485	        self,

1487	        input_deps: List[Task],

1489	    ):

1491	            runtime_ctx,
1492	            input_deps,
1493	            partition_infos,
1494	            self.npartitions,
1495	            self.dimension,

1497	            self.hive_partitioning,
1498	            self.cpu_limit,
1499	            self.memory_limit,
1500	        )

1503	def DataSetPartitionNode(
1504	    ctx: Context,
1505	    input_deps: Tuple[Node, ...],
1506	    npartitions: int,
1507	    *,
1508	    partition_by_rows=False,
1509	    random_shuffle=False,
1510	    data_partition_column=None,
1511	):
1512	    """
1513	    Partition the outputs of `input_deps` into n partitions.
1514
1515	    Parameters
1516	    ----------
1517	    npartitions
1518	        The number of partitions. The input files or rows would be evenly distributed to `npartitions` partitions.
1519	    partition_by_rows, optional
1520	        Evenly distribute rows instead of input files into `npartitions` partitions, by default distribute by files.
1521	    random_shuffle, optional
1522	        Random shuffle the list of paths or parquet row groups (if `partition_by_rows=True`) in input datasets.
1523	    data_partition_column, optional
1524	        Partition by files based on the partition keys stored in `data_partition_column` if specified.
1525	        Default column name used by `HashPartitionNode` is `DATA_PARTITION_COLUMN_NAME`.
1526
1527	    Examples
1528	    --------
1529	    See unit test `test_load_partitioned_datasets` in `test/test_partition.py`.
1530	    """
1531	    assert not (partition_by_rows and data_partition_column), "partition_by_rows and data_partition_column cannot be set at the same time"
1532	    if data_partition_column is None:
1533	        partition_node = EvenlyDistributedPartitionNode(
1534	            ctx,
1535	            input_deps,
1536	            npartitions,
1537	            dimension=None,
1538	            nested=False,
1539	            partition_by_rows=partition_by_rows,
1540	            random_shuffle=random_shuffle,
1541	        )
1542	        if npartitions == 1:
1543	            return ConsolidateNode(ctx, partition_node, dimensions=[])
1544	        else:
1545	            return partition_node
1546	    else:
1547	        return LoadPartitionedDataSetNode(
1548	            ctx,
1549	            input_deps,
1550	            npartitions,
1551	            dimension=data_partition_column,
1552	            nested=False,
1553	            data_partition_column=data_partition_column,
1554	            hive_partitioning=False,
1555	        )
1556
1557
1558	class HashPartitionNode(PartitionNode):
1559	    """
1560	    Partition the outputs of `input_deps` into n partitions based on the hash values of `hash_columns`.
1561	    """
1562
1563	    default_cpu_limit = 1
1564	    default_memory_limit = None
1565	    default_data_partition_column = DATA_PARTITION_COLUMN_NAME
1566	    default_engine_type = "duckdb"
1567	    default_row_group_size = DEFAULT_ROW_GROUP_SIZE
1568	    max_num_producer_tasks = 1000
1569	    enable_resource_boost = True
1570
1571	    def __init__(
1572	        self,
1573	        ctx: Context,
1574	        input_deps: Tuple[Node, ...],
1575	        npartitions: int,
1576	        hash_columns: List[str] = None,
1577	        data_partition_column: str = None,
1578	        *,
1579	        dimension: str = None,
1580	        nested: bool = False,
1581	        engine_type: Literal["duckdb", "arrow"] = None,
1582	        random_shuffle: bool = False,
1583	        shuffle_only: bool = False,
1584	        drop_partition_column: bool = False,
1585	        use_parquet_writer: bool = False,
1586	        hive_partitioning: bool = False,
1587	        parquet_row_group_size: int = None,
1588	        parquet_dictionary_encoding=False,
1589	        parquet_compression="ZSTD",
1590	        parquet_compression_level=3,
1591	        output_name: str = None,
1592	        output_path: str = None,
1593	        cpu_limit: Optional[int] = None,
1594	        memory_limit: Optional[int] = None,
1595	    ) -> None:
1596	        """
1597	        Construct a HashPartitionNode. See :func:`Node.__init__` to find comments on other parameters.
1598
1599	        Parameters
1600	        ----------
1601	        npartitions
1602	            The number of hash partitions. The number of generated parquet files would be proportional to `npartitions`.
1603	        hash_columns
1604	            The hash values are computed from `hash_columns`.
1605	        data_partition_column, optional
1606	            The name of column used to store partition keys.
1607	        engine_type, optional
1608	            The underlying query engine for hash partition.
1609	        random_shuffle, optional
1610	            Ignore `hash_columns` and shuffle each row to a random partition if true.
1611	        shuffle_only, optional
1612	            Ignore `hash_columns` and shuffle each row to the partition specified in `data_partition_column` if true.
1613	        drop_partition_column, optional
1614	            Exclude `data_partition_column` in output if true.
1615	        use_parquet_writer, optional
1616	            Convert partition data to arrow tables and append with parquet writer if true. This creates less number of
1617	            intermediate files but makes partitioning slower.
1618	        hive_partitioning, optional
1619	            Use Hive partitioned write of duckdb if true.
1620	        parquet_row_group_size, optional
1621	            The number of rows stored in each row group of parquet file.
1622	            Large row group size provides more opportunities to compress the data.
1623	            Small row groups size could make filtering rows faster and achieve high concurrency.
1624	            See https://duckdb.org/docs/data/parquet/tips.html#selecting-a-row_group_size.
1625	        parquet_dictionary_encoding, optional
1626	            Specify if we should use dictionary encoding in general or only for some columns.
1627	            See `use_dictionary` in https://arrow.apache.org/docs/python/generated/pyarrow.parquet.ParquetWriter.html.
1628	        """
1629	        assert not random_shuffle or not shuffle_only, f"random_shuffle and shuffle_only cannot be enabled at the same time"
1630	        assert not shuffle_only or data_partition_column is not None, f"data_partition_column not specified for shuffle-only partitioning"
1631	        assert data_partition_column is None or re.match(
1632	            "[a-zA-Z0-9_]+", data_partition_column
1633	        ), f"data_partition_column has invalid format: {data_partition_column}"
1634	        assert engine_type in (
1635	            None,
1636	            "duckdb",
1637	            "arrow",
1638	        ), f"unknown query engine type: {engine_type}"
1639	        data_partition_column = data_partition_column or self.default_data_partition_column
1640	        super().__init__(
1641	            ctx,
1642	            input_deps,
1643	            npartitions,
1644	            dimension or data_partition_column,
1645	            nested,
1646	            output_name,
1647	            output_path,
1648	            cpu_limit or self.default_cpu_limit,
1649	            memory_limit or self.default_memory_limit,
1650	        )
1651	        self.hash_columns = ["random()"] if random_shuffle else hash_columns
1652	        self.data_partition_column = data_partition_column
1653	        self.engine_type = engine_type or self.default_engine_type
1654	        self.random_shuffle = random_shuffle
1655	        self.shuffle_only = shuffle_only
1656	        self.drop_partition_column = drop_partition_column
1657	        self.use_parquet_writer = use_parquet_writer
1658	        self.hive_partitioning = hive_partitioning and self.engine_type == "duckdb"
1659	        self.parquet_row_group_size = parquet_row_group_size or self.default_row_group_size
1660	        self.parquet_dictionary_encoding = parquet_dictionary_encoding
1661	        self.parquet_compression = parquet_compression
1662	        self.parquet_compression_level = parquet_compression_level
1663
1664	    def __str__(self) -> str:
1665	        return (
1666	            super().__str__()
1667	            + f", hash_columns={self.hash_columns}, data_partition_column={self.data_partition_column}, engine_type={self.engine_type}, hive_partitioning={self.hive_partitioning}"
1668	        )
1669
1670	    @Node.task_factory
1671	    def create_producer_task(
1672	        self,
1673	        runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext,
1674	        input_deps: List[Task],
1675	        partition_infos: List[PartitionInfo],
1676	    ) -> HashPartitionTask:
1677	        return HashPartitionTask.create(
1678	            self.engine_type,
1679	            runtime_ctx,
1680	            input_deps,
1681	            partition_infos,
1682	            self.npartitions,
1683	            self.dimension,
1684	            self.hash_columns,
1685	            self.data_partition_column,
1686	            self.random_shuffle,
1687	            self.shuffle_only,
1688	            self.drop_partition_column,
1689	            self.use_parquet_writer,
1690	            self.hive_partitioning,
1691	            self.parquet_row_group_size,
1692	            self.parquet_dictionary_encoding,
1693	            self.parquet_compression,
1694	            self.parquet_compression_level,
1695	            self.output_name,
1696	            self.output_path,
1697	            self.cpu_limit,
1698	            self.memory_limit,
1699	        )
1700

1749	class RangePartitionNode(PartitionNode):
1750	    """

1752	    """

1755	        self,

1780	class ProjectionNode(Node):
1781	    """
1782	    Select columns from output of an input node.
1783	    """
1784
1785	    def __init__(
1786	        self,
1787	        ctx: Context,
1788	        input_dep: Node,
1789	        columns: List[str] = None,
1790	        generated_columns: List[Literal["filename", "file_row_number"]] = None,
1791	        union_by_name=None,
1792	    ) -> None:
1793	        """
1794	        Construct a ProjectNode to select only the `columns` from output of `input_dep`.
1795
1796	        Parameters
1797	        ----------
1798	        input_dep
1799	            The input node whose output would be selected.
1800	        columns, optional
1801	            The columns to be selected or created. Select all columns if set to `None`.
1802	        generated_columns
1803	            Auto generated columns, supported values: `filename`, `file_row_number`.
1804	        union_by_name, optional
1805	            Unify the columns of different files by name (see https://duckdb.org/docs/data/multiple_files/combining_schemas#union-by-name).
1806
1807	        Examples
1808	        --------
1809	        First create an ArrowComputeNode to extract hosts from urls.
1810
1811	        .. code-block:: python
1812
1813	            class ParseUrl(ArrowComputeNode):
1814	                def process(self, runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext, input_tables: List[arrow.Table]) -> arrow.Table:
1815	                    assert input_tables[0].column_names == ["url"] # check url is the only column in table
1816	                    urls, = input_tables[0].columns
1817	                    hosts = [url.as_py().split("/", maxsplit=2)[0] for url in urls]
1818	                    return arrow.Table.from_arrays([hosts, urls], names=["host", "url"])
1819
1820	        Suppose there are several columns in output of `data_partitions`,
1821	        `ProjectionNode(..., ["url"])` selects the `url` column.
1822	        Then only this column would be loaded into arrow table when feeding data to `ParseUrl`.
1823
1824	        .. code-block:: python
1825
1826	            urls_with_host = ParseUrl(ctx, (ProjectionNode(ctx, data_partitions, ["url"]),))
1827	        """
1828	        columns = columns or ["*"]
1829	        generated_columns = generated_columns or []
1830	        assert all(col in GENERATED_COLUMNS for col in generated_columns), f"invalid values found in generated columns: {generated_columns}"
1831	        assert not (set(columns) & set(generated_columns)), f"columns {columns} and generated columns {generated_columns} share common columns"
1832	        super().__init__(ctx, [input_dep])
1833	        self.columns = columns
1834	        self.generated_columns = generated_columns
1835	        self.union_by_name = union_by_name
1836
1837	    def __str__(self) -> str:
1838	        return super().__str__() + f", columns={self.columns}, generated_columns={self.generated_columns}, union_by_name={self.union_by_name}"
1839
1840	    @Node.task_factory
1841	    def create_task(
1842	        self,
1843	        runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext,
1844	        input_deps: List[Task],
1845	        partition_infos: List[PartitionInfo],
1846	    ) -> ProjectionTask:
1847	        return ProjectionTask(
1848	            runtime_ctx,
1849	            input_deps,
1850	            partition_infos,
1851	            self.columns,
1852	            self.generated_columns,
1853	            self.union_by_name,
1854	        )
1855
1856
1857	class LimitNode(SqlEngineNode):
1858	    """
1859	    Limit the number of rows of the output of an input node.
1860	    """
1861
1862	    def __init__(self, ctx: Context, input_dep: Node, limit: int) -> None:
1863	        """
1864	        Construct a LimitNode to limit the number of rows of the output of `input_dep`.
1865
1866	        Parameters
1867	        ----------
1868	        input_dep
1869	            The input node whose output would be limited.
1870	        limit
1871	            The number of rows to be limited.
1872	        """
1873	        super().__init__(ctx, (input_dep,), f"select * from {{0}} limit {limit}")
1874	        self.limit = limit
1875
1876	    def __str__(self) -> str:
1877	        return super().__str__() + f", limit={self.limit}"
1878
1879	    @Node.task_factory
1880	    def create_merge_task(
1881	        self,
1882	        runtime_ctx: RuntimeContext,
1883	        input_deps: List[Task],
1884	        partition_infos: List[PartitionInfo],
1885	    ) -> MergeDataSetsTask:
1886	        return MergeDataSetsTask(runtime_ctx, input_deps, partition_infos)
1887
1888
1889	T = TypeVar("T")
1890
1891
1892	class LogicalPlanVisitor(Generic[T]):
1893	    """
1894	    Visit the nodes of a logcial plan in depth-first order.
1895	    """
1896
1897	    def visit(self, node: Node, depth: int = 0) -> T:
1898	        """
1899	        Visit a node depending on its type.
1900	        If the method for the node type is not implemented, call `generic_visit`.
1901	        """
1902	        if isinstance(node, DataSourceNode):
1903	            return self.visit_data_source_node(node, depth)
1904	        elif isinstance(node, DataSinkNode):
1905	            return self.visit_data_sink_node(node, depth)
1906	        elif isinstance(node, RootNode):
1907	            return self.visit_root_node(node, depth)
1908	        elif isinstance(node, UnionNode):
1909	            return self.visit_union_node(node, depth)
1910	        elif isinstance(node, ConsolidateNode):
1911	            return self.visit_consolidate_node(node, depth)
1912	        elif isinstance(node, PartitionNode):
1913	            return self.visit_partition_node(node, depth)
1914	        elif isinstance(node, PythonScriptNode):
1915	            return self.visit_python_script_node(node, depth)
1916	        elif isinstance(node, ArrowComputeNode):
1917	            return self.visit_arrow_compute_node(node, depth)
1918	        elif isinstance(node, ArrowStreamNode):
1919	            return self.visit_arrow_stream_node(node, depth)
1920	        elif isinstance(node, LimitNode):
1921	            return self.visit_limit_node(node, depth)
1922	        elif isinstance(node, SqlEngineNode):
1923	            return self.visit_query_engine_node(node, depth)
1924	        elif isinstance(node, ProjectionNode):
1925	            return self.visit_projection_node(node, depth)
1926	        else:
1927	            raise Exception(f"Unknown node type: {node}")
1928
1929	    def generic_visit(self, node: Node, depth: int) -> T:
1930	        """This visitor calls visit() on all children of the node."""
1931	        for dep in node.input_deps:
1932	            self.visit(dep, depth + 1)
1933
1934	    def visit_data_source_node(self, node: DataSourceNode, depth: int) -> T:
1935	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1936
1937	    def visit_data_sink_node(self, node: DataSinkNode, depth: int) -> T:
1938	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1939
1940	    def visit_root_node(self, node: RootNode, depth: int) -> T:
1941	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1942
1943	    def visit_union_node(self, node: UnionNode, depth: int) -> T:
1944	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1945
1946	    def visit_consolidate_node(self, node: ConsolidateNode, depth: int) -> T:
1947	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1948
1949	    def visit_partition_node(self, node: PartitionNode, depth: int) -> T:
1950	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1951
1952	    def visit_python_script_node(self, node: PythonScriptNode, depth: int) -> T:
1953	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1954
1955	    def visit_arrow_compute_node(self, node: ArrowComputeNode, depth: int) -> T:
1956	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1957
1958	    def visit_arrow_stream_node(self, node: ArrowStreamNode, depth: int) -> T:
1959	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1960
1961	    def visit_query_engine_node(self, node: SqlEngineNode, depth: int) -> T:
1962	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1963
1964	    def visit_projection_node(self, node: ProjectionNode, depth: int) -> T:
1965	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1966
1967	    def visit_limit_node(self, node: LimitNode, depth: int) -> T:
1968	        return self.generic_visit(node, depth)
1969
1970
1971	class LogicalPlan(object):
1972	    """
1973	    The logical plan that defines a directed acyclic computation graph.
1974	    """
1975
1976	    def __init__(self, ctx: Context, root_node: Node) -> None:
1977	        self.ctx = ctx
1978	        self.root_node = root_node
1979
1980	    def __str__(self) -> str:
1981	        return self.explain_str()
1982
1983	    def explain_str(self) -> str:
1984	        """
1985	        Return a string that shows the structure of the logical plan.
1986	        """
1987	        visited = set()
1988
1989	        def to_str(node: Node, depth: int = 0) -> List[str]:
1990	            lines = ["  " * depth + str(node) + ", file= " + node.location]
1991	            if node.id in visited:
1992	                return lines + ["  " * depth + " (omitted ...)"]
1993	            visited.add(node.id)
1994	            lines += ["  " * depth + f" | {name}: {stats}" for name, stats in node.perf_stats.items()]
1995	            for dep in node.input_deps:
1996	                lines.extend(to_str(dep, depth + 1))
1997	            return lines
1998
1999	        return os.linesep.join(to_str(self.root_node))
2000
2001	    def graph(self) -> Digraph:
2002	        """
2003	        Return a graphviz graph that shows the structure of the logical plan.
2004	        """
2005	        dot = Digraph(comment="smallpond")
2006	        for node in self.nodes.values():
2007	            dot.node(str(node.id), repr(node))
2008	            for dep in node.input_deps:
2009	                dot.edge(str(dep.id), str(node.id))
2010	        return dot
2011
2012	    @property
2013	    def nodes(self) -> Dict[NodeId, Node]:
2014	        nodes = {}
2015
2016	        def collect_nodes(node: Node):
2017	            if node.id in nodes:
2018	                return
2019	            nodes[node.id] = node
2020	            for dep in node.input_deps:
2021	                collect_nodes(dep)
2022
2023	        collect_nodes(self.root_node)
2024	        return nodes
2025

32	magic_check = re.compile(r"([*?]|\[.*\])")
33	magic_check_bytes = re.compile(rb"([*?]|\[.*\])")
34
35
36	def has_magic(s):
37	    if isinstance(s, bytes):
38	        match = magic_check_bytes.search(s)
39	    else:
40	        match = magic_check.search(s)
41	    return match is not None

44	class DataSet(object):
45	    """
46	    The base class for all datasets.
47	    """
48
49	    __slots__ = (
50	        "paths",
51	        "root_dir",
52	        "recursive",
53	        "columns",
54	        "__dict__",
55	        "_union_by_name",
56	        "_resolved_paths",
57	        "_absolute_paths",
58	        "_resolved_num_rows",
59	    )
60
61	    def __init__(
62	        self,
63	        paths: Union[str, List[str]],
64	        root_dir: Optional[str] = "",
65	        recursive=False,
66	        columns: Optional[List[str]] = None,
67	        union_by_name=False,
68	    ) -> None:
69	        """
70	        Construct a dataset from a list of paths.
71
72	        Parameters
73	        ----------
74	        paths
75	            A path or a list of paths or path patterns.
76	            e.g. `['data/100.parquet', '/datasetA/*.parquet']`.
77	        root_dir, optional
78	            Relative paths in `paths` would be resolved under `root_dir` if specified.
79	        recursive, optional
80	            Resolve path patterns recursively if true.
81	        columns, optional
82	            Only load the specified columns if not None.
83	        union_by_name, optional
84	            Unify the columns of different files by name (see https://duckdb.org/docs/data/multiple_files/combining_schemas#union-by-name).
85	        """
86	        self.paths = [paths] if isinstance(paths, str) else paths
87	        "The paths to the dataset files."
88	        self.root_dir = os.path.abspath(root_dir) if root_dir is not None else None
89	        "The root directory of paths."
90	        self.recursive = recursive
91	        "Whether to resolve path patterns recursively."
92	        self.columns = columns
93	        "The columns to load from the dataset files."
94	        self._union_by_name = union_by_name
95	        self._resolved_paths: List[str] = None
96	        self._absolute_paths: List[str] = None
97	        self._resolved_num_rows: int = None
98
99	    def __str__(self) -> str:
100	        return f"{self.__class__.__name__}: paths[{len(self.paths)}]={self.paths[:3]}...', root_dir={self.root_dir}, columns={self.columns}"
101
102	    __repr__ = __str__
103
104	    @property
105	    def _resolved_path_str(self) -> str:
106	        return ", ".join(map(lambda x: f"'{x}'", self.resolved_paths))
107
108	    @property
109	    def _column_str(self) -> str:
110	        """
111	        A column string used in SQL select clause.
112	        """
113	        return ", ".join(self.columns) if self.columns else "*"
114
115	    @property
116	    def union_by_name(self) -> bool:
117	        """
118	        Whether to unify the columns of different files by name.
119	        """
120	        return self._union_by_name or self.columns is not None
121
122	    @property
123	    def udfs(self) -> List[UDFContext]:
124	        return []
125
126	    @staticmethod
127	    def merge(datasets: "List[DataSet]") -> "DataSet":
128	        """
129	        Merge multiple datasets into a single dataset.
130	        """
131	        raise NotImplementedError
132
133	    def reset(
134	        self,
135	        paths: Optional[List[str]] = None,
136	        root_dir: Optional[str] = "",
137	        recursive=None,
138	    ) -> None:
139	        """
140	        Reset the dataset with new paths, root_dir, and recursive flag.
141	        """
142	        self.partition_by_files.cache_clear()
143	        self.paths = paths or []
144	        self.root_dir = os.path.abspath(root_dir) if root_dir is not None else None
145	        self.recursive = recursive if recursive is not None else self.recursive
146	        self._resolved_paths = None
147	        self._absolute_paths = None
148	        self._resolved_num_rows = None
149
150	    @property
151	    def num_files(self) -> int:
152	        """
153	        The number of files in the dataset.
154	        """
155	        return len(self.resolved_paths)
156
157	    @property
158	    def num_rows(self) -> int:
159	        """
160	        The number of rows in the dataset.
161	        """
162	        if self._resolved_num_rows is None:
163	            sql_query = f"select count(*) from {self.sql_query_fragment()}"
164	            row = duckdb.sql(sql_query).fetchone()
165	            assert row is not None, "no rows returned"
166	            self._resolved_num_rows = row[0]
167	        return self._resolved_num_rows
168
169	    @property
170	    def empty(self) -> bool:
171	        """
172	        Whether the dataset is empty.
173	        """
174	        if self._resolved_paths is not None:
175	            return len(self._resolved_paths) == 0
176	        for path in self.paths:
177	            if has_magic(path):
178	                if any(
179	                    glob.iglob(
180	                        os.path.join(self.root_dir or "", path),
181	                        recursive=self.recursive,
182	                    )
183	                ):
184	                    return False
185	            else:
186	                return False
187	        return True
188
189	    @property
190	    def resolved_paths(self) -> List[str]:
191	        """
192	        An ordered list of absolute paths of files.
193	        File patterns are expanded to absolute paths.
194
195	        Example::
196	        >>> DataSet(['data/100.parquet', '/datasetA/*.parquet']).resolved_paths
197	        ['/datasetA/1.parquet', '/datasetA/2.parquet', '/home/user/data/100.parquet']
198	        """
199	        if self._resolved_paths is None:
200	            resolved_paths = []
201	            wildcard_paths = []
202	            for path in self.absolute_paths:
203	                if has_magic(path):
204	                    wildcard_paths.append(path)
205	                else:
206	                    resolved_paths.append(path)
207	            if wildcard_paths:
208	                if len(wildcard_paths) == 1:
209	                    expanded_paths = glob.glob(wildcard_paths[0], recursive=self.recursive)
210	                else:
211	                    logger.debug(
212	                        "resolving {} paths with wildcards in {}",
213	                        len(wildcard_paths),
214	                        self,
215	                    )
216	                    with ThreadPoolExecutor(min(32, len(wildcard_paths))) as pool:
217	                        expanded_paths = [
218	                            p
219	                            for paths in pool.map(
220	                                lambda p: glob.glob(p, recursive=self.recursive),
221	                                wildcard_paths,
222	                            )
223	                            for p in paths
224	                        ]
225	                resolved_paths.extend(expanded_paths)
226	                logger.debug(
227	                    "resolved {} files from {} wildcard path(s) in {}",
228	                    len(expanded_paths),
229	                    len(wildcard_paths),
230	                    self,
231	                )
232	            self._resolved_paths = sorted(resolved_paths)
233	        return self._resolved_paths
234
235	    @property
236	    def absolute_paths(self) -> List[str]:
237	        """
238	        An ordered list of absolute paths of the given file patterns.
239
240	        Example::
241	        >>> DataSet(['data/100.parquet', '/datasetA/*.parquet']).absolute_paths
242	        ['/datasetA/*.parquet', '/home/user/data/100.parquet']
243	        """
244	        if self._absolute_paths is None:
245	            if self.root_dir is None:
246	                self._absolute_paths = sorted(self.paths)
247	            else:
248	                self._absolute_paths = [os.path.join(self.root_dir, p) for p in sorted(self.paths)]
249	        return self._absolute_paths
250
251	    def sql_query_fragment(
252	        self,
253	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
254	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
255	    ) -> str:
256	        """
257	        Return a sql fragment that represents the dataset.
258	        """
259	        raise NotImplementedError
260
261	    def log(self, num_rows=200):
262	        """
263	        Log the dataset to the logger.
264	        """
265	        import pandas as pd
266
267	        pd.set_option("display.max_columns", None)  # Show all columns
268	        pd.set_option("display.max_rows", None)  # Optionally show all rows
269	        pd.set_option("display.max_colwidth", None)  # No truncation of column contents
270	        pd.set_option("display.expand_frame_repr", False)  # Do not wrap rows
271	        logger.info("{} ->\n{}", self, self.to_pandas().head(num_rows))
272
273	    def to_pandas(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
274	        """
275	        Convert the dataset to a pandas dataframe.
276	        """
277	        return self.to_arrow_table().to_pandas()
278
279	    def to_arrow_table(
280	        self,
281	        max_workers: int = 16,
282	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
283	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
284	    ) -> arrow.Table:
285	        """
286	        Load the dataset to an arrow table.
287
288	        Parameters
289	        ----------
290	        max_workers, optional
291	            The maximum number of worker threads to use. Default to 16.
292	        filesystem, optional
293	            If provided, use the filesystem to load the dataset.
294	        conn, optional
295	            A duckdb connection. If provided, use duckdb to load the dataset.
296	        """
297	        sql_query = f"select {self._column_str} from {self.sql_query_fragment(filesystem, conn)}"
298	        if conn is not None:
299	            return conn.sql(sql_query).fetch_arrow_table()
300	        else:
301	            return duckdb.sql(sql_query).fetch_arrow_table()
302
303	    def to_batch_reader(
304	        self,
305	        batch_size: int = DEFAULT_BATCH_SIZE,
306	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
307	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
308	    ) -> arrow.RecordBatchReader:
309	        """
310	        Return an arrow record batch reader to read the dataset.
311
312	        Parameters
313	        ----------
314	        batch_size, optional
315	            The record batch size. Default to 122880.
316	        filesystem, optional
317	            If provided, use the filesystem to load the dataset.
318	        conn, optional
319	            A duckdb connection. If provided, use duckdb to load the dataset.
320	        """
321	        sql_query = f"select {self._column_str} from {self.sql_query_fragment(filesystem, conn)}"
322	        if conn is not None:
323	            return conn.sql(sql_query).fetch_arrow_reader(batch_size)
324	        else:
325	            return duckdb.sql(sql_query).fetch_arrow_reader(batch_size)
326
327	    def _init_file_partitions(self, npartition: int) -> "List[DataSet]":
328	        """
329	        Return `npartition` empty datasets.
330	        """
331	        file_partitions = []
332	        for _ in range(npartition):
333	            empty_dataset = copy.copy(self)
334	            empty_dataset.reset()
335	            file_partitions.append(empty_dataset)
336	        return file_partitions
337
338	    @functools.lru_cache
339	    def partition_by_files(self, npartition: int, random_shuffle: bool = False) -> "List[DataSet]":
340	        """
341	        Evenly split into `npartition` datasets by files.
342	        """
343	        assert npartition > 0, f"npartition has negative value: {npartition}"
344	        if npartition > self.num_files:
345	            logger.debug(f"number of partitions {npartition} is greater than the number of files {self.num_files}")
346
347	        resolved_paths = random.sample(self.resolved_paths, len(self.resolved_paths)) if random_shuffle else self.resolved_paths
348	        evenly_split_groups = split_into_rows(resolved_paths, npartition)
349	        num_paths_in_groups = list(map(len, evenly_split_groups))
350
351	        file_partitions = self._init_file_partitions(npartition)
352	        for i, paths in enumerate(evenly_split_groups):
353	            file_partitions[i].reset(paths, None)
354
355	        logger.debug(
356	            f"created {npartition} file partitions (min #files: {min(num_paths_in_groups)}, max #files: {max(num_paths_in_groups)}, avg #files: {sum(num_paths_in_groups)/len(num_paths_in_groups):.3f}) from {self}"
357	        )
358	        return random.sample(file_partitions, len(file_partitions)) if random_shuffle else file_partitions
359
360
361	class PartitionedDataSet(DataSet):
362	    """
363	    A dataset that is partitioned into multiple datasets.
364	    """
365
366	    __slots__ = ("datasets",)
367
368	    def __init__(self, datasets: List[DataSet]) -> None:
369	        assert len(datasets) > 0, "no dataset given"
370	        self.datasets = datasets
371	        absolute_paths = [p for dataset in datasets for p in dataset.absolute_paths]
372	        super().__init__(
373	            absolute_paths,
374	            datasets[0].root_dir,
375	            datasets[0].recursive,
376	            datasets[0].columns,
377	            datasets[0].union_by_name,
378	        )
379
380	    def __getitem__(self, key: int) -> DataSet:
381	        return self.datasets[key]
382
383	    @property
384	    def udfs(self) -> List[UDFContext]:
385	        return [udf for dataset in self.datasets for udf in dataset.udfs]
386
387	    @staticmethod
388	    def merge(datasets: "List[PartitionedDataSet]") -> DataSet:
389	        # merge partitioned datasets results in an unpartitioned dataset
390	        assert all(isinstance(dataset, PartitionedDataSet) for dataset in datasets)
391	        datasets = [d for dataset in datasets for d in dataset]
392	        return datasets[0].merge(datasets)
393
394
395	class FileSet(DataSet):
396	    """
397	    A set of files.
398	    """
399
400	    @staticmethod
401	    def merge(datasets: "List[FileSet]") -> "FileSet":
402	        assert all(isinstance(dataset, FileSet) for dataset in datasets)
403	        absolute_paths = [p for dataset in datasets for p in dataset.absolute_paths]
404	        return FileSet(absolute_paths)
405
406	    def to_arrow_table(
407	        self,
408	        max_workers=16,
409	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
410	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
411	    ) -> arrow.Table:
412	        return arrow.table([self.resolved_paths], names=["resolved_paths"])
413
414	    def to_batch_reader(
415	        self,
416	        batch_size=DEFAULT_BATCH_SIZE,
417	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
418	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
419	    ) -> arrow.RecordBatchReader:
420	        return self.to_arrow_table().to_reader(batch_size)

422
423	class CsvDataSet(DataSet):
424	    """
425	    A set of csv files.
426	    """
427
428	    __slots__ = (
429	        "schema",
430	        "delim",
431	        "max_line_size",
432	        "parallel",
433	        "header",
434	    )
435
436	    def __init__(
437	        self,
438	        paths: List[str],
439	        schema: Dict[str, str],
440	        delim=",",
441	        max_line_size: Optional[int] = None,
442	        parallel=True,
443	        header=False,
444	        root_dir: Optional[str] = "",
445	        recursive=False,
446	        columns: Optional[List[str]] = None,
447	        union_by_name=False,
448	    ) -> None:
449	        super().__init__(paths, root_dir, recursive, columns, union_by_name)
450	        assert isinstance(schema, OrderedDict), f"type of csv schema is not OrderedDict: {type(schema)}"
451	        self.schema = schema
452	        self.delim = delim
453	        self.max_line_size = max_line_size
454	        self.parallel = parallel
455	        self.header = header
456
457	    @staticmethod
458	    def merge(datasets: "List[CsvDataSet]") -> "CsvDataSet":
459	        assert all(isinstance(dataset, CsvDataSet) for dataset in datasets)
460	        absolute_paths = [p for dataset in datasets for p in dataset.absolute_paths]
461	        return CsvDataSet(
462	            absolute_paths,
463	            datasets[0].schema,
464	            datasets[0].delim,
465	            datasets[0].max_line_size,
466	            datasets[0].parallel,
467	            recursive=any(dataset.recursive for dataset in datasets),
468	            columns=datasets[0].columns,
469	            union_by_name=any(dataset.union_by_name for dataset in datasets),
470	        )
471
472	    def sql_query_fragment(
473	        self,
474	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
475	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
476	    ) -> str:
477	        schema_str = ", ".join(map(lambda x: f"'{x[0]}': '{x[1]}'", self.schema.items()))
478	        max_line_size_str = f"max_line_size={self.max_line_size}, " if self.max_line_size is not None else ""
479	        return (
480	            f"( select {self._column_str} from read_csv([ {self._resolved_path_str} ], delim='{self.delim}', columns={{ {schema_str} }}, header={self.header}, "
481	            f"{max_line_size_str} parallel={self.parallel}, union_by_name={self.union_by_name}) )"
482	        )
483

537
538	class ParquetDataSet(DataSet):
539	    """
540	    A set of parquet files.
541	    """
542
543	    __slots__ = (
544	        "generated_columns",
545	        "_resolved_row_ranges",
546	    )
547
548	    def __init__(
549	        self,
550	        paths: List[str],
551	        root_dir: Optional[str] = "",
552	        recursive=False,
553	        columns: Optional[List[str]] = None,
554	        generated_columns: Optional[List[str]] = None,
555	        union_by_name=False,
556	    ) -> None:
557	        super().__init__(paths, root_dir, recursive, columns, union_by_name)
558	        self.generated_columns = generated_columns or []
559	        "Generated columns of DuckDB `read_parquet` function. e.g. `file_name`, `file_row_number`."
560	        self._resolved_row_ranges: List[RowRange] = None
561
562	    def __str__(self) -> str:
563	        s = super().__str__() + f", generated_columns={self.generated_columns}"
564	        if self._resolved_row_ranges:
565	            s += f", resolved_row_ranges[{len(self._resolved_row_ranges)}]={self._resolved_row_ranges[:3]}..."
566	        return s
567
568	    __repr__ = __str__
569
570	    @property
571	    def _column_str(self) -> str:
572	        if not self.columns:
573	            return "*"
574	        if "*" in self.columns:
575	            return ", ".join(self.columns)
576	        return ", ".join(self.columns + self.generated_columns)
577
578	    @staticmethod
579	    def merge(datasets: "List[ParquetDataSet]") -> "ParquetDataSet":
580	        assert all(isinstance(dataset, ParquetDataSet) for dataset in datasets)
581	        dataset = ParquetDataSet(
582	            paths=[p for dataset in datasets for p in dataset.absolute_paths],
583	            root_dir=None,
584	            recursive=any(dataset.recursive for dataset in datasets),
585	            columns=datasets[0].columns,
586	            generated_columns=datasets[0].generated_columns,
587	            union_by_name=any(dataset.union_by_name for dataset in datasets),
588	        )
589	        # merge row ranges if any dataset has resolved row ranges
590	        if any(dataset._resolved_row_ranges is not None for dataset in datasets):
591	            dataset._resolved_row_ranges = [row_range for dataset in datasets for row_range in dataset.resolved_row_ranges]
592	        return dataset
593
594	    @staticmethod
595	    def create_from(table: arrow.Table, output_dir: str, filename: str = "data"):
596	        dump_to_parquet_files(table, output_dir, filename)
597	        return ParquetDataSet([os.path.join(output_dir, f"{filename}*.parquet")])
598
599	    def reset(
600	        self,
601	        paths: Optional[List[str]] = None,
602	        root_dir: Optional[str] = "",
603	        recursive=None,
604	    ) -> None:
605	        """
606	        NOTE: all row ranges will be cleared. DO NOT call this if you want to keep partial files.
607	        """
608	        super().reset(paths, root_dir, recursive)
609	        self._resolved_row_ranges = None
610	        self.partition_by_files.cache_clear()
611	        self.partition_by_rows.cache_clear()
612	        self.partition_by_size.cache_clear()
613
614	    @property
615	    def resolved_row_ranges(self) -> List[RowRange]:
616	        """
617	        Return row ranges for each parquet file.
618	        """
619	        if self._resolved_row_ranges is None:
620	            if len(self.resolved_paths) == 0:
621	                self._resolved_row_ranges = []
622	            else:
623
624	                def resolve_row_range(path: str) -> RowRange:
625	                    # read parquet metadata to get number of rows
626	                    metadata = parquet.read_metadata(path)
627	                    num_rows = metadata.num_rows
628	                    uncompressed_data_size = sum(metadata.row_group(i).total_byte_size for i in range(metadata.num_row_groups))
629	                    return RowRange(
630	                        path,
631	                        data_size=uncompressed_data_size,
632	                        file_num_rows=num_rows,
633	                        begin=0,
634	                        end=num_rows,
635	                    )
636
637	                with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=min(32, len(self.resolved_paths))) as pool:
638	                    self._resolved_row_ranges = list(pool.map(resolve_row_range, self.resolved_paths))
639	        return self._resolved_row_ranges
640
641	    @property
642	    def num_rows(self) -> int:
643	        if self._resolved_num_rows is None:
644	            self._resolved_num_rows = sum(row_range.num_rows for row_range in self.resolved_row_ranges)
645	        return self._resolved_num_rows
646
647	    @property
648	    def empty(self) -> bool:
649	        # this method should be quick. do not resolve row ranges.
650	        if self._resolved_num_rows is not None or self._resolved_row_ranges is not None:
651	            return self.num_rows == 0
652	        return super().empty
653
654	    @property
655	    def estimated_data_size(self) -> int:
656	        """
657	        Return the estimated data size in bytes.
658	        """
659	        return sum(row_range.estimated_data_size for row_range in self.resolved_row_ranges)
660
661	    def sql_query_fragment(
662	        self,
663	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
664	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
665	    ) -> str:
666	        extra_parameters = "".join(f", {col}=true" for col in self.generated_columns) if self.generated_columns else ""
667	        parquet_file_queries = []
668	        full_row_ranges = []
669
670	        for row_range in self.resolved_row_ranges:
671	            path = filesystem.unstrip_protocol(row_range.path) if filesystem else row_range.path
672	            if row_range.num_rows == row_range.file_num_rows:
673	                full_row_ranges.append(row_range)
674	            else:
675	                sql_query = f"""
676	          select {self._column_str}
677	          from read_parquet('{path}' {extra_parameters}, file_row_number=true)
678	          where file_row_number between {row_range.begin} and {row_range.end - 1}
679	        """
680	                if "file_row_number" not in self.generated_columns:
681	                    sql_query = f"select columns(c -> c != 'file_row_number') from ( {sql_query} )"
682	                parquet_file_queries.append(sql_query)
683
684	        # NOTE: prefer:     read_parquet([path1, path2, ...])
685	        #       instead of: read_parquet(path1) union all read_parquet(path2) union all ...
686	        #       for performance
687	        if full_row_ranges:
688	            # XXX: duckdb uses the first file as the estimated cardinality of `read_parquet`
689	            #      to prevent incorrect estimation, we move the largest file to the head
690	            largest_index = max(
691	                range(len(full_row_ranges)),
692	                key=lambda i: full_row_ranges[i].file_num_rows,
693	            )
694	            full_row_ranges[0], full_row_ranges[largest_index] = (
695	                full_row_ranges[largest_index],
696	                full_row_ranges[0],
697	            )
698	            parquet_file_str = ",\n            ".join(map(lambda x: f"'{x.path}'", full_row_ranges))
699	            parquet_file_queries.insert(
700	                0,
701	                f"""
702	          select {self._column_str}
703	          from read_parquet([
704	            {parquet_file_str}
705	          ], union_by_name={self.union_by_name} {extra_parameters})
706	      """,
707	            )
708
709	        union_op = " union all by name " if self.union_by_name else " union all "
710	        return f"( {union_op.join(parquet_file_queries)} )"
711
712	    def to_arrow_table(
713	        self,
714	        max_workers=16,
715	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
716	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
717	    ) -> arrow.Table:
718	        if conn is not None:
719	            return super().to_arrow_table(max_workers, filesystem, conn)
720
721	        tables = []
722	        if self.resolved_row_ranges:
723	            tables.append(load_from_parquet_files(self.resolved_row_ranges, self.columns, max_workers, filesystem))
724	        return arrow.concat_tables(tables)
725
726	    def to_batch_reader(
727	        self,
728	        batch_size=DEFAULT_BATCH_SIZE,
729	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
730	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
731	    ) -> arrow.RecordBatchReader:
732	        if conn is not None:
733	            return super().to_batch_reader(batch_size, filesystem, conn)
734
735	        return build_batch_reader_from_files(
736	            self.resolved_row_ranges,
737	            columns=self.columns,
738	            batch_size=batch_size,
739	            filesystem=filesystem,
740	        )
741
742	    @functools.lru_cache
743	    def partition_by_files(self, npartition: int, random_shuffle: bool = False) -> "List[ParquetDataSet]":
744	        if self._resolved_row_ranges is not None:
745	            return self.partition_by_rows(npartition, random_shuffle)
746	        else:
747	            return super().partition_by_files(npartition, random_shuffle)
748
749	    @functools.lru_cache
750	    def partition_by_rows(self, npartition: int, random_shuffle: bool = False) -> "List[ParquetDataSet]":
751	        """
752	        Evenly split the dataset into `npartition` partitions by rows.
753	        If `random_shuffle` is True, shuffle the files before partitioning.
754	        """
755	        assert npartition > 0, f"npartition has negative value: {npartition}"
756
757	        resolved_row_ranges = self.resolved_row_ranges
758	        resolved_row_ranges = random.sample(resolved_row_ranges, len(resolved_row_ranges)) if random_shuffle else resolved_row_ranges
759
760	        def create_dataset(row_ranges: List[RowRange]) -> ParquetDataSet:
761	            row_ranges = sorted(row_ranges, key=lambda x: x.path)
762	            resolved_paths = [x.path for x in row_ranges]
763	            dataset = ParquetDataSet(
764	                resolved_paths,
765	                columns=self.columns,
766	                generated_columns=self.generated_columns,
767	                union_by_name=self.union_by_name,
768	            )
769	            dataset._resolved_paths = resolved_paths
770	            dataset._resolved_row_ranges = row_ranges
771	            return dataset
772
773	        return [create_dataset(row_ranges) for row_ranges in RowRange.partition_by_rows(resolved_row_ranges, npartition)]
774
775	    @functools.lru_cache
776	    def partition_by_size(self, max_partition_size: int) -> "List[ParquetDataSet]":
777	        """
778	        Split the dataset into multiple partitions so that each partition has at most `max_partition_size` bytes.
779	        """
780	        if self.empty:
781	            return []
782	        estimated_data_size = sum(row_range.estimated_data_size for row_range in self.resolved_row_ranges)
783	        npartition = estimated_data_size // max_partition_size + 1
784	        return self.partition_by_rows(npartition)
785
786	    @staticmethod
787	    def _read_partition_key(path: str, data_partition_column: str, hive_partitioning: bool) -> int:
788	        """
789	        Get the partition key of the parquet file.
790
791	        Examples
792	        --------
793	        ```
794	        >>> ParquetDataSet._read_partition_key("output/000.parquet", "key", hive_partitioning=False)
795	        1
796	        >>> ParquetDataSet._read_partition_key("output/key=1/000.parquet", "key", hive_partitioning=True)
797	        1
798	        ```
799	        """
800
801	        def parse_partition_key(key: str):
802	            try:
803	                return int(key)
804	            except ValueError:
805	                logger.error(f"cannot parse partition key '{data_partition_column}' of {path} from: {key}")
806	                raise
807
808	        if hive_partitioning:
809	            path_part_prefix = data_partition_column + "="
810	            for part in path.split(os.path.sep):
811	                if part.startswith(path_part_prefix):
812	                    return parse_partition_key(part[len(path_part_prefix) :])
813	            raise RuntimeError(f"cannot extract hive partition key '{data_partition_column}' from path: {path}")
814
815	        with parquet.ParquetFile(path) as file:
816	            kv_metadata = file.schema_arrow.metadata or file.metadata.metadata
817	            if kv_metadata is not None:
818	                for key, val in kv_metadata.items():
819	                    key, val = key.decode("utf-8"), val.decode("utf-8")
820	                    if key == PARQUET_METADATA_KEY_PREFIX + data_partition_column:
821	                        return parse_partition_key(val)
822	            if file.metadata.num_rows == 0:
823	                logger.warning(f"cannot read partition keys from empty parquet file: {path}")
824	                return None
825	            for batch in file.iter_batches(batch_size=128, columns=[data_partition_column], use_threads=False):
826	                assert data_partition_column in batch.column_names, f"cannot find column '{data_partition_column}' in {batch.column_names}"
827	                assert batch.num_columns == 1, f"unexpected num of columns: {batch.column_names}"
828	                uniq_partition_keys = set(batch.columns[0].to_pylist())
829	                assert uniq_partition_keys and len(uniq_partition_keys) == 1, f"partition keys found in {path} not unique: {uniq_partition_keys}"
830	                return uniq_partition_keys.pop()
831
832	    def load_partitioned_datasets(self, npartition: int, data_partition_column: str, hive_partitioning=False) -> "List[ParquetDataSet]":
833	        """
834	        Split the dataset into a list of partitioned datasets.
835	        """
836	        assert npartition > 0, f"npartition has negative value: {npartition}"
837	        if npartition > self.num_files:
838	            logger.debug(f"number of partitions {npartition} is greater than the number of files {self.num_files}")
839
840	        file_partitions: List[ParquetDataSet] = self._init_file_partitions(npartition)
841	        for dataset in file_partitions:
842	            # elements will be appended later
843	            dataset._absolute_paths = []
844	            dataset._resolved_paths = []
845	            dataset._resolved_row_ranges = []
846
847	        if not self.resolved_paths:
848	            logger.debug(f"create {npartition} empty data partitions from {self}")
849	            return file_partitions
850
851	        with ThreadPoolExecutor(min(32, len(self.resolved_paths))) as pool:
852	            partition_keys = pool.map(
853	                lambda path: ParquetDataSet._read_partition_key(path, data_partition_column, hive_partitioning),
854	                self.resolved_paths,
855	            )
856
857	        for row_range, partition_key in zip(self.resolved_row_ranges, partition_keys):
858	            if partition_key is not None:
859	                assert 0 <= partition_key <= npartition, f"invalid partition key {partition_key} found in {row_range.path}"
860	                dataset = file_partitions[partition_key]
861	                dataset.paths.append(row_range.path)
862	                dataset._absolute_paths.append(row_range.path)
863	                dataset._resolved_paths.append(row_range.path)
864	                dataset._resolved_row_ranges.append(row_range)
865
866	        logger.debug(f"loaded {npartition} data partitions from {self}")
867	        return file_partitions
868
869	    def remove_empty_files(self) -> None:
870	        """
871	        Remove empty parquet files from the dataset.
872	        """
873	        new_row_ranges = [row_range for row_range in self.resolved_row_ranges if row_range.num_rows > 0]
874	        if len(new_row_ranges) == 0:
875	            # keep at least one file to avoid empty dataset
876	            new_row_ranges = self.resolved_row_ranges[:1]
877	        if len(new_row_ranges) == len(self.resolved_row_ranges):
878	            # no empty files found
879	            return
880	        logger.info(f"removed {len(self.resolved_row_ranges) - len(new_row_ranges)}/{len(self.resolved_row_ranges)} empty parquet files from {self}")
881	        self._resolved_row_ranges = new_row_ranges
882	        self._resolved_paths = [row_range.path for row_range in new_row_ranges]
883	        self._absolute_paths = self._resolved_paths
884	        self.paths = self._resolved_paths
885
886
887	class SqlQueryDataSet(DataSet):
888	    """
889	    The result of a sql query.
890	    """
891
892	    __slots__ = (
893	        "sql_query",
894	        "query_builder",
895	    )
896
897	    def __init__(
898	        self,
899	        sql_query: str,
900	        query_builder: Callable[[duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection, fsspec.AbstractFileSystem], str] = None,
901	    ) -> None:
902	        super().__init__([])
903	        self.sql_query = sql_query
904	        self.query_builder = query_builder
905
906	    @property
907	    def num_rows(self) -> int:
908	        num_rows = duckdb.sql(f"select count(*) as num_rows from {self.sql_query_fragment()}").fetchall()
909	        return num_rows[0][0]
910
911	    def sql_query_fragment(
912	        self,
913	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
914	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
915	    ) -> str:
916	        sql_query = self.sql_query if self.query_builder is None else self.query_builder(conn, filesystem)
917	        return f"( {sql_query} )"

923	    """

930	        self,
931	        max_workers=16,
932	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
933	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
934	    ) -> arrow.Table:

937	    def to_batch_reader(
938	        self,
939	        batch_size=DEFAULT_BATCH_SIZE,
940	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
941	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
942	    ) -> arrow.RecordBatchReader:
943	        return self.table.to_reader(batch_size)
944
945	    def sql_query_fragment(
946	        self,
947	        filesystem: fsspec.AbstractFileSystem = None,
948	        conn: duckdb.DuckDBPyConnection = None,
949	    ) -> str:
950	        name = f"arrow_table_{id(self.table)}"
951	        self.table.to_pandas().to_sql(name, conn, index=False)
952	        return f"( select * from {name} )"

320	        if os.path.exists(self.job_root):
321	            if cleanup_root:
322	                remove_path(self.job_root)
323	            elif not root_exist_ok:
324	                raise FileExistsError(f"Folder already exists: {self.job_root}")
325	        os.makedirs(self.config_root, exist_ok=root_exist_ok)
326	        os.makedirs(self.queue_root, exist_ok=root_exist_ok)
327	        os.makedirs(self.output_root, exist_ok=root_exist_ok)

329	        os.makedirs(self.temp_root, exist_ok=root_exist_ok)

334	    def _init_envs(self):
335	        sys.setrecursionlimit(100000)
336	        env_overrides = copy.copy(self.env_overrides)
337	        ld_library_path = os.getenv("LD_LIBRARY_PATH", "")
338	        py_library_path = os.path.join(sys.exec_prefix, "lib")
339	        if py_library_path not in ld_library_path:
340	            env_overrides["LD_LIBRARY_PATH"] = ":".join([py_library_path, ld_library_path])
341	        for key, val in env_overrides.items():
342	            if (old := os.getenv(key, None)) is not None:
343	                logger.info(f"overwrite environment variable '{key}': '{old}' -> '{val}'")
344	            else:
345	                logger.info(f"set environment variable '{key}': '{val}'")
346	            os.environ[key] = val
347	        logger.info(
348	            f"RANK='{os.getenv('RANK', '')}' LD_LIBRARY_PATH='{os.getenv('LD_LIBRARY_PATH', '')}' LD_PRELOAD='{os.getenv('LD_PRELOAD', '')}' MALLOC_CONF='{os.getenv('MALLOC_CONF', '')}'"
349	        )

352	        log_rotation = {"rotation": "100 MB", "retention": 5} if not self.disable_log_rotation else {}

354	        user_log_only = {"": self.file_log_level, "smallpond": False}
